# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-29 22:08:37.524332

### Base Program

```py
def kthSymbolInGrammar(n, k):
    if n == 1:
        return 0
    if k % 2 == 0:
        return 1 - kthSymbolInGrammar(n - 1, k // 2)
    else:
        return kthSymbolInGrammar(n - 1, (k + 1) // 2)
```

### Input

```json
[14, 97]
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def kthSymbolInGrammar(n, k):
    if n == 1:
        return 0
    if k % 2 == 0:
        return 1 - kthSymbolInGrammar(n - 1, k // 2)
    else:
        return kthSymbolInGrammar(n - 1, (k + 1) // 2)
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def kthSymbolInGrammar(var_0, var_1):
    if var_0 == 1:
        return 0
    if var_1 % 2 == 0:
        return 1 - kthSymbolInGrammar(var_0 - 1, var_1 // 2)
    else:
        return kthSymbolInGrammar(var_0 - 1, (var_1 + 1) // 2)
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def kthSymbolInGrammar(n, k):
    if n == 1:
        return 0
    if k % 2 == 0:
        return 1 + -kthSymbolInGrammar(n + -1, k // 2)
    else:
        return kthSymbolInGrammar(n + -1, (1 + k) // 2)
```

<details>
<summary>parser endpoint: passed ✅</summary>

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def kthSymbolInGrammar(var_2, var_3):
    if var_2 == 1:
        return 0
    if var_3 % 2 == 0:
        return 1 + -kthSymbolInGrammar(var_2 + -1, var_3 // 2)
    else:
        return kthSymbolInGrammar(var_2 + -1, (1 + var_3) // 2)
```
